backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:1:# Opensearch Idiosyncrasies
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:4:Opensearch has 2 phases, a `Search` phase and a `Fetch` phase. The `Search` phase works by getting the document scores on each
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:6:an intermediate phase (seemingly built specifically to handle hybrid search queries) which can run in between as a processor.
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:8:https://docs.opensearch.org/latest/search-plugins/search-pipelines/search-processors/
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:9:https://docs.opensearch.org/latest/search-plugins/search-pipelines/normalization-processor/
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:10:https://docs.opensearch.org/latest/query-dsl/compound/hybrid/
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:12:## How Hybrid queries work
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:13:Hybrid queries are basically parallel queries that each run through their own `Search` phase and do not interact in any way.
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:17:When the normalization processor is applied to keyword/vector hybrid searches, documents that show up due to keyword match may
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:18:not also have showed up in the vector search and vice versa. In these situations, it just receives a 0 score for the missing
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:19:query component. Opensearch does not run another phase to recapture those missing values. The impact of this is that after
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:35:So these boosts can only be applied after normalization. Unfortunately with Opensearch, the normalization processor runs last
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:37:query which filters on recently updated documents) is added, it would not be able to introduce any new documents
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:38:to the set (since the new documents would have no keyword/vector score or already be present) since the 0 scores on keyword
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:39:and vector would make the docs which only came because of time filter very low scoring. This can however make some of the lower
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:43:contents. If there are lots of updates, this may miss.
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:49:So while it is possible to apply time based boosting at the normalization stage (or specifically to the keyword score), we have
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:50:decided it is better to not apply it during the OpenSearch query.
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:52:Because of these limitations, Onyx in code applies further refinements, boostings, etc. based on OpenSearch providing an initial
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:54:from OpenSearch.
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:58:work that is relevant for the hybrid search. Since the Rescore happens prior to normalization, it's not able to provide any
backend/onyx/document_index/opensearch/README.md:61:Because the Title is included in the Contents for both embedding and keyword searches, the Title scores are very low relative to
